implemented across multiple files in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository, centered around the admission.Interface abstraction and its two main implementations: MutationInterface for mutating webhooks and ValidationInterface for validating webhooks.\\n\\nCore Interface Definitions (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go):\\nThe admission system is built on the admission.Interface, which defines the Handles(operation) method to determine if a handler can process a request. MutationInterface extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admissions, and ValidationInterface provides Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validation-only admissions. The Attributes and ObjectInterfaces interfaces provide request context and object handling capabilities.\\n\\nAdmission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go):\\nThe chainAdmissionHandler is a []Interface slice that implements the admission chain pattern. It executes handlers sequentially: the Admit() method iterates through handlers calling Admit() on MutationInterface types, and Validate() iterates through handlers calling Validate() on ValidationInterface types. Both return immediately on first error.\\n\\nReinvocation Support (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go):\\nThe newReinvocationHandler() function wraps the admission chain in a reinvoker struct that implements reinvocation policies. The reinvoker's Admit() method checks if re-invocation is needed after the initial admission phase and reinvokes the chain if required. This allows mutating webhooks to be re-run if earlier mutations require validation of modified objects.\\n\\nPlugin Management and Chain Building (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go):\\nThe Plugins type manages plugin registration and instantiation. The NewFromPlugins() method builds the complete admission chain by: (1) iterating through plugin names, (2) instantiating each plugin, (3) separating plugins into mutation and validation lists, (4) wrapping handlers with optional decorators, and (5) wrapping the final chain with newReinvocationHandler(). This method returns the wrapped chain.\\n\\nPlugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go and pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go):\\nRegisterAllAdmissionPlugins() registers both generic plugins (lifecycle, mutating/validating webhooks, policies) and kube-apiserver specific plugins. The registration order is irrelevant at registration time but execution order is strictly controlled: all mutating plugins run before validating plugins.\\n\\nAdmission Options and Configuration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go):\\nAdmissionOptions holds plugin names, configuration file path, and decorators. The ApplyTo() method is responsible for: (1) reading plugin configuration, (2) creating plugin initializers, (3) building the admission chain via Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), (4) wrapping with metrics via WithStepMetrics(), and (5) storing in server config as AdmissionControl.\\n\\nMutating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\nThe mutating Plugin implements admission.MutationInterface. Register() adds it to the plugins registry. NewMutatingWebhook() instantiates it with a handler and dispatcher. The Admit() method delegates to the generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes configured MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects in deterministic order via mutatingDispatcher.\\n\\nValidating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\nThe validating Plugin implements admission.ValidationInterface with similar structure to mutating webhooks. NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook() creates it with a dispatcher. The Validate() method delegates to generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects via validatingDispatcher.\\n\\nWebhook Dispatchers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and validating/dispatcher.go):\\nmutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher implement the generic.Dispatcher interface. They manage webhook execution, including handling re-invocation contexts, applying patches (for mutating), and enforcing failure policies. They work with WebhookAccessors obtained from configuration managers.\\n\\nWebhook Configuration Managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\nmutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager manage dynamic webhook configurations. They list and cache MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects respectively, ensuring deterministic ordering and efficient recompilation of webhook policies.\\n\\nDecorators and Wrappers:\\nThe decorator.Decorator interface allows wrapping handlers with additional behavior. WithAudit() (audit.go) wraps handlers to log admission annotations to audit events. WithStepMetrics() (metrics/metrics.go) instruments admission with prometheus metrics. These are applied via the Decorators slice in NewFromPlugins().\\n\\nRequest Handling Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/):\\nIn create.go, update.go, delete.go, and rest.go, handlers check if admit is a MutationInterface and call Admit(), then check if it's ValidationInterface and call Validate(). The admission chain is invoked after authorization but before persistence, with attributes like operation type (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT), request object, old object (for updates), and user info.\\n\\nExecution Flow Summary:\\n1. Client request arrives at API server\\n2. Authentication and authorization complete\\n3. Request body deserialized\\n4. AdmissionControl interface (the wrapped chain) is invoked\\n5. Mutating phase: chainAdmissionHandler.Admit() runs all mutating plugins/webhooks in order\\n6. Reinvocation check: if mutations occurred, reinvoker may reinvoke the chain\\n7. Validating phase: chainAdmissionHandler.Validate() runs all validating plugins/webhooks\\n8. If any handler rejects, request fails; otherwise proceeds to persistence\\n\\nThe admission system achieves its goals through this layered architecture: the Interface abstraction allows pluggability, chainAdmissionHandler provides sequential execution, reinvoker handles re-invocation policies, decorators add cross-cutting concerns (audit, metrics), and webhook dispatchers manage dynamic configuration of MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook resources.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":833,"cache_read_input_tokens":95018,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":833},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"581a479b-cfb0-4528-a6cf-e01c71908419","uuid":"3aa8a504-dfad-46ad-8b9c-a35738c71a10"}

This method returns the wrapped chain.\\n\\nPlugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go and pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go):\\nRegisterAllAdmissionPlugins() registers both generic plugins (lifecycle, mutating/validating webhooks, policies) and kube-apiserver specific plugins. The registration order is irrelevant at registration time but execution order is strictly controlled: all mutating plugins run before validating plugins.\\n\\nAdmission Options and Configuration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go):\\nAdmissionOptions holds plugin names, configuration file path, and decorators. The ApplyTo() method is responsible for: (1) reading plugin configuration, (2) creating plugin initializers, (3) building the admission chain via Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), (4) wrapping with metrics via WithStepMetrics(), and (5) storing in server config as AdmissionControl.\\n\\nMutating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\nThe mutating Plugin implements admission.MutationInterface. Register() adds it to the plugins registry. NewMutatingWebhook() instantiates it with a handler and dispatcher. The Admit() method delegates to the generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes configured MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects in deterministic order via mutatingDispatcher.\\n\\nValidating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\nThe validating Plugin implements admission.ValidationInterface with similar structure to mutating webhooks. NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook() creates it with a dispatcher. The Validate() method delegates to generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects via validatingDispatcher.\\n\\nWebhook Dispatchers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and validating/dispatcher.go):\\nmutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher implement the generic.Dispatcher interface. They manage webhook execution, including handling re-invocation contexts, applying patches (for mutating), and enforcing failure policies. They work with WebhookAccessors obtained from configuration managers.\\n\\nWebhook Configuration Managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\nmutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager manage dynamic webhook configurations. They list and cache MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects respectively, ensuring deterministic ordering and efficient recompilation of webhook policies.\\n\\nDecorators and Wrappers:\\nThe decorator.Decorator interface allows wrapping handlers with additional behavior. WithAudit() (audit.go) wraps handlers to log admission annotations to audit events. WithStepMetrics() (metrics/metrics.go) instruments admission with prometheus metrics. These are applied via the Decorators slice in NewFromPlugins().\\n\\nRequest Handling Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/):\\nIn create.go, update.go, delete.go, and rest.go, handlers check if admit is a MutationInterface and call Admit(), then check if it's ValidationInterface and call Validate(). The admission chain is invoked after authorization but before persistence, with attributes like operation type (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT), request object, old object (for updates), and user info.\\n\\nExecution Flow Summary:\\n1. Client request arrives at API server\\n2. Authentication and authorization complete\\n3. Request body deserialized\\n4. AdmissionControl interface (the wrapped chain) is invoked\\n5. Mutating phase: chainAdmissionHandler.Admit() runs all mutating plugins/webhooks in order\\n6. Reinvocation check: if mutations occurred, reinvoker may reinvoke the chain\\n7. Validating phase: chainAdmissionHandler.Validate() runs all validating plugins/webhooks\\n8. If any handler rejects, request fails; otherwise proceeds to persistence\\n\\nThe admission system achieves its goals through this layered architecture: the Interface abstraction allows pluggability, chainAdmissionHandler provides sequential execution, reinvoker handles re-invocation policies, decorators add cross-cutting concerns (audit, metrics), and webhook dispatchers manage dynamic configuration of MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook resources.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

is implemented across multiple files in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository, centered around the admission.Interface abstraction and its two main implementations: MutationInterface for mutating webhooks and ValidationInterface for validating webhooks.\\n\\nCore Interface Definitions (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go):\\nThe admission system is built on the admission.Interface, which defines the Handles(operation) method to determine if a handler can process a request. MutationInterface extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admissions, and ValidationInterface provides Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validation-only admissions. The Attributes and ObjectInterfaces interfaces provide request context and object handling capabilities.\\n\\nAdmission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go):\\nThe chainAdmissionHandler is a []Interface slice that implements the admission chain pattern. It executes handlers sequentially: the Admit() method iterates through handlers calling Admit() on MutationInterface types, and Validate() iterates through handlers calling Validate() on ValidationInterface types. Both return immediately on first error.\\n\\nReinvocation Support (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go):\\nThe newReinvocationHandler() function wraps the admission chain in a reinvoker struct that implements reinvocation policies. The reinvoker's Admit() method checks if re-invocation is needed after the initial admission phase and reinvokes the chain if required. This allows mutating webhooks to be re-run if earlier mutations require validation of modified objects.\\n\\nPlugin Management and Chain Building (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go):\\nThe Plugins type manages plugin registration and instantiation. The NewFromPlugins() method builds the complete admission chain by: (1) iterating through plugin names, (2) instantiating each plugin, (3) separating plugins into mutation and validation lists, (4) wrapping handlers with optional decorators, and (5) wrapping the final chain with newReinvocationHandler(). This method returns the wrapped chain.\\n\\nPlugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go and pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go):\\nRegisterAllAdmissionPlugins() registers both generic plugins (lifecycle, mutating/validating webhooks, policies) and kube-apiserver specific plugins. The registration order is irrelevant at registration time but execution order is strictly controlled: all mutating plugins run before validating plugins.\\n\\nAdmission Options and Configuration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go):\\nAdmissionOptions holds plugin names, configuration file path, and decorators. The ApplyTo() method is responsible for: (1) reading plugin configuration, (2) creating plugin initializers, (3) building the admission chain via Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), (4) wrapping with metrics via WithStepMetrics(), and (5) storing in server config as AdmissionControl.\\n\\nMutating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\nThe mutating Plugin implements admission.MutationInterface. Register() adds it to the plugins registry. NewMutatingWebhook() instantiates it with a handler and dispatcher. The Admit() method delegates to the generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes configured MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects in deterministic order via mutatingDispatcher.\\n\\nValidating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\nThe validating Plugin implements admission.ValidationInterface with similar structure to mutating webhooks. NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook() creates it with a dispatcher. The Validate() method delegates to generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects via validatingDispatcher.\\n\\nWebhook Dispatchers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and validating/dispatcher.go):\\nmutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher implement the generic.Dispatcher interface. They manage webhook execution, including handling re-invocation contexts, applying patches (for mutating), and enforcing failure policies. They work with WebhookAccessors obtained from configuration managers.\\n\\nWebhook Configuration Managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\nmutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager manage dynamic webhook configurations. They list and cache MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects respectively, ensuring deterministic ordering and efficient recompilation of webhook policies.\\n\\nDecorators and Wrappers:\\nThe decorator.Decorator interface allows wrapping handlers with additional behavior. WithAudit() (audit.go) wraps handlers to log admission annotations to audit events. WithStepMetrics() (metrics/metrics.go) instruments admission with prometheus metrics. The admission chain is invoked after authorization but before persistence, with attributes like operation type (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT), request object, old object (for updates), and user info.\\n\\nExecution Flow Summary:\\n1. Client request arrives at API server\\n2. Authentication and authorization complete\\n3. Request body deserialized\\n4. AdmissionControl interface (the wrapped chain) is invoked\\n5. implemented across multiple files in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository, centered around the admission.Interface abstraction and its two main implementations: MutationInterface for mutating webhooks and ValidationInterface for validating webhooks.\\n\\nCore Interface Definitions (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go):\\nThe admission system is built on the admission.Interface, which defines the Handles(operation) method to determine if a handler can process a request. MutationInterface extends Interface with Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for mutating admissions, and ValidationInterface provides Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) for validation-only admissions. The Attributes and ObjectInterfaces interfaces provide request context and object handling capabilities.\\n\\nAdmission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go):\\nThe chainAdmissionHandler is a []Interface slice that implements the admission chain pattern. It executes handlers sequentially: the Admit() method iterates through handlers calling Admit() on MutationInterface types, and Validate() iterates through handlers calling Validate() on ValidationInterface types. Both return immediately on first error.\\n\\nReinvocation Support (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go):\\nThe newReinvocationHandler() function wraps the admission chain in a reinvoker struct that implements reinvocation policies. The reinvoker's Admit() method checks if re-invocation is needed after the initial admission phase and reinvokes the chain if required. This allows mutating webhooks to be re-run if earlier mutations require validation of modified objects.\\n\\nPlugin Management and Chain Building (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go):\\nThe Plugins type manages plugin registration and instantiation. The NewFromPlugins() method builds the complete admission chain by: (1) iterating through plugin names, (2) instantiating each plugin, (3) separating plugins into mutation and validation lists, (4) wrapping handlers with optional decorators, and (5) wrapping the final chain with newReinvocationHandler(). This method returns the wrapped chain.\\n\\nPlugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go and pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go):\\nRegisterAllAdmissionPlugins() registers both generic plugins (lifecycle, mutating/validating webhooks, policies) and kube-apiserver specific plugins. The registration order is irrelevant at registration time but execution order is strictly controlled: all mutating plugins run before validating plugins.\\n\\nAdmission Options and Configuration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go):\\nAdmissionOptions holds plugin names, configuration file path, and decorators. The ApplyTo() method is responsible for: (1) reading plugin configuration, (2) creating plugin initializers, (3) building the admission chain via Plugins.NewFromPlugins(), (4) wrapping with metrics via WithStepMetrics(), and (5) storing in server config as AdmissionControl.\\n\\nMutating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\nThe mutating Plugin implements admission.MutationInterface. Register() adds it to the plugins registry. NewMutatingWebhook() instantiates it with a handler and dispatcher. The Admit() method delegates to the generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes configured MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects in deterministic order via mutatingDispatcher.\\n\\nValidating Admission Webhooks (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\nThe validating Plugin implements admission.ValidationInterface with similar structure to mutating webhooks. NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook() creates it with a dispatcher. The Validate() method delegates to generic Webhook's Dispatch() which invokes ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects via validatingDispatcher.\\n\\nWebhook Dispatchers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and validating/dispatcher.go):\\nmutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher implement the generic.Dispatcher interface. They manage webhook execution, including handling re-invocation contexts, applying patches (for mutating), and enforcing failure policies. They work with WebhookAccessors obtained from configuration managers.\\n\\nWebhook Configuration Managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\nmutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager manage dynamic webhook configurations. They list and cache MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects respectively, ensuring deterministic ordering and efficient recompilation of webhook policies.\\n\\nDecorators and Wrappers:\\nThe decorator.Decorator interface allows wrapping handlers with additional behavior. WithAudit() (audit.go) wraps handlers to log admission annotations to audit events. WithStepMetrics() (metrics/metrics.go) instruments admission with prometheus metrics. These are applied via the Decorators slice in NewFromPlugins().\\n\\nRequest Handling Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/):\\nIn create.go, update.go, delete.go, and rest.go, handlers check if admit is a MutationInterface and call Admit(), then check if it's ValidationInterface and call Validate(). The admission chain is invoked after authorization but before persistence, with attributes like operation type (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT), request object, old object (for updates), and user info.\\n\\nExecution Flow Summary:\\n1. Client request arrives at API server\\n2. Authentication and authorization complete\\n3. Request body deserialized\\n4. AdmissionControl interface (the wrapped chain) is invoked\\n5. Mutating phase: chainAdmissionHandler.Admit() runs all mutating plugins/webhooks in order\\n6. Reinvocation check: if mutations occurred, reinvoker may reinvoke the chain\\n7. Validating phase: chainAdmissionHandler.Validate() runs all validating plugins/webhooks\\n8. If any handler rejects, request fails; otherwise proceeds to persistence\\n\\nThe admission system achieves its goals through this layered architecture: the Interface abstraction allows pluggability, chainAdmissionHandler provides sequential execution, reinvoker handles re-invocation policies, decorators add cross-cutting concerns (audit, metrics), and webhook dispatchers manage dynamic configuration of MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook resources.\"\n}\n","numLines":77,"startLine":1,"totalLines":77}}}
